#### 4-year Plan
event = {
	id = 9300001
	country = GER
	random = no

	decision = { atwar = no ideology = nazi or = { event = 2003135 year = 1937 } } # Unemployment down to 5%
	decision_trigger = { money = 1000 minister = 58 } # Goering as MoA
	trigger = { or = { event = 2003135 year = 1937 } atwar = no ideology = nazi random = 50 }

	name = "9300001name"
	desc = "9300001desc"
	style = 2
	picture = "Four_Year"
	decision_picture = "decision_Four_Year"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 180
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }
	
	action = {
		ai_chance = 30
		name = "9300001a"
		command = { type = building_prod_mod which = ic value = 10 }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 5210 } } type = gain_tech which = 5210 } # Oil Refining 1940
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 5220 } } type = gain_tech which = 5220 } # Oil Refining 1941
		command = { type = domestic which = free_market value = -1 } # Autarky
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 56 } # Schacht
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -1000 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 40
		name = "9300001b"
    		command = { type = build_time which = armor when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -10 }
      		command = { type = build_time which = light_armor when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -10 }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2650 } } type = gain_tech which = 2650 } # L ARM 1934
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2030 } } type = gain_tech which = 2030 } # L ARM 1936
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2040 } } type = gain_tech which = 2040 } # L ARM 1938
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2050 } } type = gain_tech which = 2050 } # L ARM 1939
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2070 } } type = gain_tech which = 2070 } # ARM 1939
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 56 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -1000 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 20
		name = "9300001c"
      		command = { type = build_time which = air when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -10 }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 4400 } } type = gain_tech which = 4400 } # CAS 1934
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 4170 } } type = gain_tech which = 4170 } # CAS 1937
	   	# command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 4280 } } type = gain_tech which = 4280 } # CAS 1940
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 4140 } } type = gain_tech which = 4140 } # TAC 1938
	   	# command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 4150 } } type = gain_tech which = 4150 } # TAC 1940
		# command = { type = event which = 9300075 where = -1 when = 90 }
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 56 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -1000 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 10
		name = "9300001d"
      		command = { type = build_time which = naval when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -10 }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 3660 } } type = gain_tech which = 3660 } # SUB 1937
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 3670 } } type = gain_tech which = 3670 } # SUB 1940
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 3260 } } type = gain_tech which = 3260 } # CA 1934
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 3340 } } type = gain_tech which = 3340 } # BC 1934
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 56 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -1000 }
	}
}


#### Polish Campaign Goals
event = {
	id = 9300002
	country = GER

	trigger = { ai = no war = { country = GER country = POL } not = { control = { province = 232 data = GER } losses = 50000 } event = 2003036 } # Danzig or War

	name = 9300002name
	desc = 9300002desc 
	style = 2
	picture = "Hitler_Staff"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }
	
	action = {
		name = 9300002a # Let us gamble!
		command = { type = event which = 9300003 where = -1 when = 30 }
	}
	action = {
		name = 9300002b # I don't feel confident
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 9300046 } # 88 mm as Ground Troops Support
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 9300211 } # Knight's Cross of the Iron Cross
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 9300300 } # Sturmgeschütz III Development
	}
}
event = {
	id = 9300003
	country = GER

	name = 9300002name
	desc = 9300003desc
	style = 2
	picture = "Hitler_Staff"
	
	action = {
		trigger = { not = { losses = 50000 } control = { province = 232 data = GER } }
		name = 9300003a
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
		command = { type = supplies value = 5000 }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2320 } } type = gain_tech which = 2320 } # ART 1938
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2330 } } type = gain_tech which = 2330 } # ART 1940
	}
	action = {
		trigger = { or = { losses = 50000 not = { control = { province = 232 data = GER } } } }
		name = 9300003b
		command = { type = dissent value = 2 }
	}
}

	id = 9300164
	random = no
	country = SOV

	trigger = { ideology = stalinist atwar = no random = 5 }

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 60
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	name = 9300164name
	desc = 9300164desc
	style = 2

	picture = "Stakhanov"
	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_GREAT
		command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = total value = 0.01 }
	}
}

# Align Portugal
event = {
	id = 9300175
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = {
		event = 2003047 # German diplomatic offensive
		exists = POR
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = POR country = GER } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = POR country = ENG } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = GER } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = ITA } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = SPA } }
	}

	decision_trigger = {
	 	relation = { which = POR value = 100 }
		alliance = { country = SPA country = GER }
		control = { province = 348 data = -3 }	# Gibraltar
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 453 type = land size = 1 area = 1 }  # Caceres
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 450 type = land size = 1 area = 1 }  # Plasencia
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 447 type = land size = 1 area = 1 }  # Salamanca
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 458 type = land size = 1 area = 1 }  # Badajoz
}

	trigger = {
		alliance = { country = SPA country = GER }
		random = 10
		exists = POR
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = POR country = GER } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = POR country = ENG } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = GER } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = ITA } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = SPA } }
	}

	name = 9300175name
	desc = 9300175desc
  	style = 2
  	picture = "hungary_axis"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300176 }
	}
}

# Hitler Declares War Against the USA
event = {
	id = 9300346
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = { 
			event = 2011025 
			NOT = { war = { country = USA } alliance = { country = USA } war = { country = JAP } } 
			war = { country = USA country = JAP } 
			event = 2011004 
			} # Anti-Comintern Pact + Pearl Harbor
	decision_trigger = { }
	trigger = { event = 2011025 NOT = { war = { country = USA } alliance = { country = USA } war = { country = JAP } } war = { country = USA country = JAP } event = 2011004 } # Anti-Comintern Pact + Pearl Harbor

	date = { year = 1933 month = january day = 1 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { year = 1999 month = december day = 29 }

   	name = 9300346name
	desc = 9300346desc
	style = 2
	picture = "Reichstag"
	decision_picture = "decision_Reichstag"

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_GREAT
		command = { type = war which = USA }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 8620 } } type = gain_tech which = 8620 } # Wolfpacks (1940)
      		command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
		command = { type = relation which = JAP value = 100 }
    		command = { type = task_efficiency which = convoy_raiding value = 0.1 }
		command = { type = event which = 9300400 where = -1 when = 150 }
	}
}

# Initiate Diplomatic Talks with Ireland
event = {
	id = 9300347
	random = no
	country = ENG

	decision = { 
			war = { country = GER } 
			not = { alliance = { country = IRE } } 
			control = { province = 55 data = -3 } 
			headofgovernment = 10017 
			} # Paris
	decision_trigger = { money = 100 }
	trigger = { war = { country = GER } not = { alliance = { country = IRE } } control = { province = 55 data = -3 } headofgovernment = 10017 random = 20 } # Paris

	date = { year = 1933 month = january day = 1 }
	offset = 60
	deathdate = { year = 1999 month = december day = 29 }

   	name = 9300347name
	desc = 9300347desc
	style = 2
	picture = "diplomatic_campaign"
	decision_picture = "decision_diplomatic_campaign"

	action = {
		ai_chance = 80
		name = 9300347a # Ports Access
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300348 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 20
		name = 9300347b # Full-Alliance and Ulster Returns
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300349 }
	}
}
event = {
	id = 9300348
	random = no
	country = IRE

   	name = 9300348name
	desc = 9300347desc
	style = 2
	picture = "diplomatic_campaign"

	action = {
		ai_chance = 40
		name = 9300348a
		command = { type = access which = ENG }
		command = { type = relation which = ENG value = 20 }
      		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = dissent value = 5 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 60
		name = 9300348b
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300349 }
	}
}

	id = 9300349

	}

	}
}

###############
# Prepare Seelöwe
event = {
	id = 9300351
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = { 
			war = { country = ENG } 
			control = { province = 55 data = -3 } 
			control = { province = 29 data = -2 } 
			not = { war = { country = SOV } } 
		} # Paris & London
	decision_trigger = { supplies = 1000 }
	trigger = { war = { country = ENG } control = { province = 55 data = -3 } control = { province = 29 data = -2 } not = { war = { country = SOV } } } # Paris & London

	date = { year = 1933 month = january day = 1 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { year = 1999 month = december day = 29 }

   	name = 9300351name
	desc = 9300351desc
	style = 2
	picture = "Hitler_Staff"
	decision_picture = "decision_Warsaw_Bombing"

	action = {
		ai_chance = 100
		name = 9300351a # Air Superiority First
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 9190 } } type = gain_tech which = 9190 } # First Strike Doctrine (1940)
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 9240 } } type = gain_tech which = 9240 } # Formation Fighting Doctrine (1940)
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 9260 } } type = gain_tech which = 9260 } # Recon Skirmisher Doctrine (1940)
      		command = { type = task_efficiency which = naval_strike value = 0.1 }
      		command = { type = task_efficiency which = convoy_air_raiding value = 0.1 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = supplies value = -1000 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 0
		name = 9300351b # Prepare Landing
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 82310 } } type = gain_tech which = 82310 } # Naval Invasion (1934)
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 82320 } } type = gain_tech which = 82320 } # Naval Invasion (1938)
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 1560 } } type = gain_tech which = 1560 } # Marines (1922)
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 1580 } } type = gain_tech which = 1580 } # Marines (1925)
	  	command = { type = task_efficiency which = amphibious_assault value = 0.1 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = supplies value = -1000 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 9300208 } # The Blitz
	}
	action = { trigger = { not = { war = { country = IRE } } }
		ai_chance = 0
		name = 9300351c # Prepare Invasion of Ireland (Fall Green)
		command = { type = war which = IRE }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 9190 } } type = gain_tech which = 9190 } # First Strike Doctrine (1940)
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 9240 } } type = gain_tech which = 9240 } # Formation Fighting Doctrine (1940)
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 82310 } } type = gain_tech which = 82310 } # Naval Invasion (1934)
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 1560 } } type = gain_tech which = 1560 } # Marines (1922)
      		command = { type = task_efficiency which = naval_strike value = 0.05 }
      		command = { type = task_efficiency which = convoy_air_raiding value = 0.05 }
	  	command = { type = task_efficiency which = amphibious_assault value = 0.05 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = supplies value = -1000 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 9300208 } # The Blitz
	}
}

# Stalin's Organ
event = {
	id = 9300108
	random = no
	country = SOV
	
	name = 9300108name
	desc = 9300108desc
	style = 2
	picture = "Stalin_Organ"

	trigger = { 
		war = { country = SOV country = GER }
		random = 30
	}

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 60
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_GREAT
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2970 } } type = gain_tech which = 2970 } # R ART 1940
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2370 } } type = gain_tech which = 2370 } # R ART 1942
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300109 }
	}
}

# Hobart's Funnies
event = {
	id = 9300284
	random = no
	country = ENG

	decision = {
		year = 1943
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
		control = { province = 29 data = -3 } # London
		control = { province = 163 data = -2 } # Berlin
		control = { province = 55 data = -2 } # Paris
	}
	
	decision_trigger = { 
		supplies = 500 
	}	
	
	trigger = {
		year = 1943
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
		control = { province = 29 data = -3 } # London
		control = { province = 163 data = -2 } # Berlin
		control = { province = 55 data = -2 } # Paris
		random = 30
	}

	name = 9300284name
	desc = 9300284desc
	style = 2
	picture = "Hobarts_Funnies"
	decision_picture = "decision_Hobarts_Funnies"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_GREAT
      	command = { type = build_time which = amph_armor when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -10 }
		command = { type = add_leader_skill which = 10134 value = 1 } # Hobart
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = supplies value = -500 }
	}
}

# Create the Decima Flottiglia MAS
event = {
	id = 9300355
	random = no
	country = ITA

	decision = { 
		technology = 1560 # Marines 1922
	}	
	decision_trigger = { 
		technology = 1570 # Marines 1925
		money = 50
		supplies = 100
	}	
	trigger = { 
		technology = 1570 # Marines 1925
		random = 20
	}	

   	name = 9300355name	
	desc = 9300355desc	
	style = 2	
	picture = "Frogmen"
	decision_picture = "decision_Frogmen"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }	
	offset = 60	
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }	

	action = {	
		name = ACTION_NAME_GREAT
		command = { type = river_attack which = infantry value = 2 }
		command = { type = shore_attack which = infantry value = 2 }
		command = { type = build_time which = infantry value = 4 when = on_upgrade }
		command = { type = river_attack which = marine value = 2 }
		command = { type = shore_attack which = marine value = 2  }
		command = { type = build_time which = marine value = 4 when = on_upgrade }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -50 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = supplies value = -100 }
	}
}
